MONSTERS - 

Here is the combined and fixed numbered list of all the monsters you provided:

1. **The Sylvan Juggernaut**
* **Role:** Heavy Tank / Environmental Hazard
* **Appearance:** A massive, hulking bipedal beast that has completely merged with its forest environment. Its primary defense is a thick, naturally regenerating layer of dense tree bark armor. Its eyes glow with a dim, mossy light from deep within a wooden carapace.
* **Mechanics:**
* **Ablative Armor:** The tree bark armor must be shattered by heavy attacks or fire magic before players can deal damage to its actual health pool.
* **Rooting Strike:** It slams its massive fists into the ground, causing roots to burst upward, briefly immobilizing players caught in the area of effect.
* **Regrowth:** If left alone for too long, it will root itself and slowly regenerate its bark plating.




2. **The Scrap-Stalker**
* **Role:** High-Mobility Assassin / Flanker
* **Appearance:** A predatory, canine-like creature that has been augmented with scavenged technology. It features asymmetrical mechanical limb elements—such as a hydraulic hind leg for massive leaping power or a bladed prosthetic forelimb. Exposed wires and raw muscle weave together under a patchy coat.
* **Mechanics:**
* **Hydraulic Pounce:** Uses its mechanical leg to close distances instantly, pinning an isolated player.
* **Overclock:** At 30% health, its mechanical parts surge with electricity, increasing its attack speed and movement speed drastically, but causing it to take slight damage over time.
* **EMP Howl:** A short-range area-of-effect ability that temporarily disables player abilities or HUD elements.




3. **The Nexus Swarmers (Evolutionary Threat)**
* **Role:** Mob / Escalating Threat
* **Appearance:** Small, glowing, crystalline parasites that hover just off the ground. Individually, they look like fragile geometric shapes with a single, scanning eye.
* **Mechanics:**
* **Swarm Mentality:** They attack in clusters, dealing very little damage alone but easily overwhelming players in large numbers.
* **Adaptive Evolution:** If three or more Swarmers survive a skirmish for more than 30 seconds, they fuse together to evolve into a Nexus Warden—a larger, humanoid crystalline construct with long-range beam attacks and heavier defenses. Players must prioritize clearing them quickly to prevent this evolution.




4. **The Void Anomaly**
* **Role:** Elite / Mini-Boss
* **Appearance:** A glitching, shifting silhouette that doesn't quite belong in the game's reality. It looks like a humanoid figure constantly phasing between different states of matter, trailing dark, wispy energy.
* **Mechanics:**
* **Phase Shift:** It can momentarily become intangible, allowing player attacks to pass right through it while it repositions.
* **Reality Tear:** Tears a temporary rift in the battlefield that slowly pulls players toward it, dealing damage to anyone who touches the center.




5. **The Tremor-Fiend (The Rhythm Disruptor)**
* **Role:** Area Denial / Pacing Dictator
* **Appearance:** A hulking, subterranean amphibian with large, resonant sacs on its throat and heavy, mallet-like forelimbs. It radiates a constant, low-frequency hum.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **The Metronome Strike:** Instead of fast swipes, it slams its limbs into the ground on a strict, predictable rhythm, sending out radial shockwaves. Players must time their evasive flips or aerial combos to the "beat" of the shockwaves to avoid losing their combo multiplier.
* **Sonic Bellow:** An unblockable, cone-shaped attack telegraphed by its throat sacs expanding and glowing. Players cannot counter this; they must use a directional dodge or vault over another enemy to clear the blast zone.




6. **The Iron-Jaw Hound (The Grappler)**
* **Role:** Combo Breaker / Priority Target
* **Appearance:** A heavily muscled, quadrupedal beast with a massive, reinforced jaw designed to latch onto its prey and never let go. It stays low to the ground, pacing around the edges of the melee.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **The Latch:** It doesn't swipe; it lunges. If a player fails to execute a perfect counter, the Hound locks its jaws onto the player's arm or leg, instantly halting the free-flow state and draining health over time.
* **Ally Assist:** In an online setting, if a teammate is grappled, another player can perform a specialized "vault-kick" off the beast to instantly break the hold and seamlessly continue their own combo chain.




7. **The Aegis Carapace (The Wall)**
* **Role:** Directional Blocker
* **Appearance:** An insectoid creature boasting a massive, impenetrable shell on its front, resembling a walking riot shield. Its vulnerable abdomen is only exposed from the rear or above.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **Deflection:** Standard frontal strikes will bounce off, immediately breaking the player's flow and causing a brief stagger.
* **Vault-Over Vulnerability:** Players must identify the Aegis in the crowd, sprint toward it, and use a specific "vault" maneuver to leap over its head, striking its exposed back mid-air before landing into a new combo against surrounding enemies.




8. **The Venom-Spitter (The Sniper)**
* **Role:** Ranged Harasser / Flow Extender
* **Appearance:** A fragile, serpentine creature that clings to walls or hovers on the periphery of the combat arena, avoiding direct melee engagement.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **Telegraphed Projectiles:** It spits globes of corrosive acid, preceded by a bright, distinct visual flash (e.g., a yellow indicator icon) and an audible hiss.
* **Projectile Reversal:** If the player hits the counter button at the exact moment the acid is about to strike, they fluidly spin and bat the projectile back at the Spitter, instantly neutralizing the threat without having to break away from the main melee brawl.




9. **The Gnarl-Maws (The Heavy-Chewers)**
* **Role:** Fodder / Movement Restrictor
* **Appearance:** Squat, blocky beasts with thick, leathery hides and massively overdeveloped jaws. They look like they were built purely to gnaw through solid steel and refuse to let go.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **The Latch & Drag:** Instead of striking, they throw themselves at the player's legs or weapons. They deal very little damage, but if one latches on, the player's movement and attack speed are significantly reduced.
* **Shake-Off:** The player must execute a specific heavy slam attack or a rapid ground-sweep to dislodge them. Because they are incredibly durable for their size, they act as damage sponges that require a sustained flurry of hits to permanently put down.




10. **The Grid-Rushers (The Wave Fodder)**
* **Role:** Combo-Batteries / Positional Threat
* **Appearance:** Spindly, glowing automatons or feral insects that move with absolute, single-minded forward momentum.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **Linear Swarm:** Acting almost like a living wave in a defense game, they have zero self-preservation and rush the player in overwhelming, predictable straight lines.
* **One-Hit Wonders:** They die in a single strike. Their purpose isn't to be a tough fight, but to flood the arena. The player must use wide, sweeping Area-of-Effect (AoE) attacks to clear the lanes. Highly skilled players will actively seek them out just to artificially inflate their combo multiplier before unleashing a finisher on a bigger boss.




11. **The Scrap-Phalanx (The Clumper)**
* **Role:** Defensive Horde
* **Appearance:** Weak, fragile scavengers or drones that carry large, jagged pieces of metal debris, rusted car doors, or thick wood planks over their heads.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **The Turtle Shell:** Individually, they are completely useless. However, their AI tells them to instantly clump together in tight packs, forming a makeshift, multi-directional wall of junk that blocks standard light attacks.
* **Scatter Strike:** The player cannot punch through the shield wall from the ground. They must use the free-flow system to launch themselves into the air and execute a vertical dive-bomb attack into the center of the pack, shattering the debris and scattering the exposed, highly vulnerable enemies underneath.




12. **The Siphon-Ticks (The Meter Drainers)**
* **Role:** Evasive Nuisance / Priority Target
* **Appearance:** Small, skittering, tick-like creatures that naturally camouflage with the floor of the arena. They have glowing, translucent abdomens.
* **Free-Flow Mechanics:**
* **The Opportunist:** They actively avoid the main brawl. However, if the player is knocked down or briefly staggered by a larger enemy, the Ticks dart in, steal a chunk of the player's combo meter or special ability energy, and immediately flee toward the edge of the map.
* **The Chase:** The player must briefly ignore the large threats and use swift traversal mechanics (like a grapple or a long-distance vault) to chase down the fleeing Tick and squash it to reclaim their stolen energy.


BOSSES - 

1. The Ascendant Colossus
Role: Multi-Phase Titan / Form-Shifter
Appearance: A towering, primeval giant that dramatically alters its physical form and elemental typing as the fight progresses. It undergoes complete structural evolutions mid-fight, drastically changing its silhouette and attack patterns.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

Evolutionary Phases: It begins as a slow, heavily armored stone giant requiring the player to use heavy combo finishers to chip away armor plating. At 50% health, its outer shell shatters, evolving into a pure energy or lightning-based entity. This forces the player to instantly switch from a heavy-brawling style to a highly evasive, counter-attack-focused rhythm.

Structural Scaling: Ground strikes are ineffective against its sheer size. The player must use their free-flow traversal abilities to grapple onto the boss, smoothly transitioning their ground combos into aerial strikes while climbing its limbs to reach weak points.

2. The Syndicate Lich
Role: Undead Commander / Zone Controller
Appearance: A skeletal, regal figure floating above the battlefield, surrounded by dark, swirling magic. It acts more like a battlefield general or a ruthless mob boss than a standard spellcaster.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

Issuing Orders: The Lich rarely dirties its own hands. Instead, it issues distinct, highly visible "orders" to specific undead minions or anomalies on the battlefield. For example, it might command a heavy bruiser to detonate. The player must quickly redirect their free-flow combo to vault across the arena and intercept the marked target before the order is executed.

Combo-Locked Shielding: The Lich is protected by an impenetrable barrier. The only way to shatter the barrier is by maintaining a continuous, unbroken 50-hit combo on the surrounding horde. If the player's combo meter resets, the Lich's shield instantly regenerates.

3. The Resonant Behemoth
Role: Rhythm-Based Giant / Environmental Hazard
Appearance: A colossal, subterranean beast with glowing, crystalline structures along its spine that vibrate with intense, bone-rattling low frequencies.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

The Bass Drop: The giant charges a massive, arena-wide shockwave that makes the floor completely lethal for several seconds. To survive, the player must launch a smaller enemy into the air and perform an extended, mid-air juggle combo, using the enemy as a springboard to stay entirely off the ground until the vibration ends.

Echo Strikes: Its physical slams leave behind a delayed, secondary impact in the exact same spot. Players cannot just dodge and counter from where they stand; they must execute continuous lateral vaults, constantly staying one step ahead of the trailing shockwaves while keeping their combo alive.

1. The Null Anomaly
Role: Reality Warper / Precision Tester
Appearance: A glitching, shifting humanoid figure composed of fragmented digital light and void energy. It never quite looks solid, constantly stuttering through the environment like a corrupted file in reality.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

Echo Splintering: Instead of dodging, it splits into three or four identical "echoes" that surround the player. Only one is real. If the player strikes a fake echo, their combo instantly shatters and they are briefly stunned. The player must spot a subtle visual tell (e.g., the real one casts a shadow, or its core glows a specific color) and seamlessly direct their combo toward the correct target.

Gravity Reversal: It temporarily flips the gravity of the arena. The player must instantly transition from ground-based brawling to an aerial juggle system, using floating debris to vault between enemies while suspended in the air.

2. The Apex Chimera
Role: Evolutionary Beast / Mob Integrator
Appearance: A massive, biomechanical predator with a highly unstable genetic structure. It features exposed integration ports and synthetic muscle fibers, looking like a terrifying blend of organic beast and hyper-advanced machinery.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

Forced Evolution: The Chimera doesn't just summon low-level fodder; it actively tries to consume them. If it grabs a smaller mob, it instantly evolves a new weapon on its body (e.g., eating a ranged mob gives it a plasma cannon on its shoulder; eating a heavy mob gives it a reinforced tail club).

Interception Combos: To stop it from evolving into an unstoppable force, the player has to physically intercept the mobs being pulled toward the boss. This forces a frantic, highly mobile playstyle where the player uses grapple strikes to rip fodder away from the boss's mouth, keeping their combo alive by bouncing between the boss and its food.

3. The Resonance Maestro
Role: Sonic Spellcaster / Tempo Controller
Appearance: An eccentric, hovering spellcaster adorned in heavily stylized, almost festival-like armor. It carries massive tuning forks instead of a staff and attacks using concentrated, visible waves of heavy bass and sound.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

The Bass Trap: The Maestro fires slow-moving, massive spheres of sonic energy that bounce around the arena. Hitting one directly breaks your combo and blasts you backward. However, the player can use a specific "redirect counter" to hit a sphere at the exact right frame, turning it into a projectile that tracks back to the boss.

Tempo Shift: As its health drops, the Maestro literally changes the tempo of the fight. The attack indicators, the movement speed of the boss, and the parry windows all speed up or slow down to match a new rhythm. The player cannot rely on muscle memory alone; they must actively listen and watch to adapt their button presses to the new beat.


1. The Data-Forged Evolvarch
Role: Evolutionary Titan / Form-Shifter
Appearance: A massive, towering beast composed of shifting, glowing code and heavy metallic armor plating. It feels inherently digital, as if its biology is constantly being rewritten in real-time.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

Tiered Evolution: It doesn't just gain a new attack phase; its physical form completely restructures through distinct evolutionary stages. It might start as a heavily armored quadruped (requiring heavy, charged strikes to break its guard) and rapidly evolve into a sleek, winged biped (forcing the player to use grapple mechanics and aerial juggles).

Evolution Interrupt: Periodically, it will encase itself in a protective data-ring to begin its next evolution. To prevent it from reaching its final, devastating "mega" state, players must aggressively chain an unbroken, high-hit combo on the data-ring to shatter it and force the boss to remain in its current, weaker form.

2. The Ivory Behemoth
Role: Charging Giant / Positioning Test
Appearance: A gargantuan, ancient pachyderm with sweeping, multi-pronged tusks and skin like cracked, hardened earth. It is a pure, unstoppable force of nature.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

The Stampede: The Behemoth charges relentlessly across the arena. Standard strikes and blocks do absolutely nothing against its mass. The player must wait for the exact parry window, fluidly vault over its sweeping tusks, and chain strikes on its exposed back while it crashes into the arena walls.

Parasitic Swarm: As the Behemoth takes damage, it shakes off swarms of smaller, aggressive parasites that cling to its legs. The player must seamlessly weave their ground combos between dodging the Behemoth's massive stomps and clearing the fodder enemies to maintain their combo multiplier.

3. The Astral Sovereign
Role: Cosmic Lich / Gravity Manipulator
Appearance: A skeletal, ethereal figure suspended in a vacuum of dark space-dust and shattered orbital debris. It wears tattered, regal robes that seem to absorb the light around it, wielding the raw, crushing power of the cosmos.
Free-Flow Mechanics:

Zero-G Combos: At set intervals, the Sovereign suspends the entire arena in zero gravity. The player's free-flow movement completely changes, allowing them to dash between floating pieces of debris and execute infinitely chaining, frictionless aerial strikes without ever touching the floor.

Orbital Deflection: The Lich pulls condensed meteors and astral debris from the sky, hurling them at the player. The player must use perfectly timed counter-attacks to physically roundhouse-kick or bat the smaller space debris back into the Lich's cosmic shield to crack it open, allowing them to close the distance for a melee flurry.


MONSTER/BOSS STATS - 

# Comprehensive Bestiary & Boss Stats

**Stat Glossary:**
*   **HP (Health Points):** The raw damage threshold required to eliminate the enemy.
*   **STR (Strength):** Physical and elemental damage output per successful strike (1 - 100).
*   **SPD (Speed):** Movement velocity, evasion capability, and attack animation speed (1 - 100).
*   **DEF (Defense):** Armor integrity, stagger resistance, and overall damage mitigation (1 - 100).
*   **ACC (Accuracy):** Hit-chance and tracking capability against a player's dodges or vaults (1 - 100).
*   **MAG (Magnetism):** The aggro threshold. High MAG means the enemy actively hunts the player; low MAG means they maintain distance or flee (1 - 100).

*   **STR:** 85 - 95 (Unstoppable force of nature)
*   **SPD:** 70 - 85 (Relentless charging speed)

*   **ACC:** 40 - 60
*   **MAG:** 95 - 100 (Constantly targets the player with its stampede)

**2. The Resonant Behemoth (Level 8 Milestone)**

CLASSES - 

1. The Protocol Weaver
Combat Style: Reality Manipulation / Crowd Control

Free-Flow Mechanic: This class fights by analyzing and "editing" the battlefield. Instead of raw physical strikes, they use spatial anomalies to restructure the fight. A perfect parry allows them to "revise" an enemy's state, stripping away armor or reversing their attack vectors. High-level combos allow them to temporarily erase low-level fodder from the combat zone entirely to focus on priority targets.

Class 1 Architecture: The Protocol Weaver
The master of battlefield manipulation, turning physical combat into an exercise of structural and cognitive analysis.

Sub-Class 1: The EPI-Savant (Focuses on extreme structural manipulation of the enemy and predicting behavioral patterns).

Specialization A: Structural Revision (Shattering enemy armor, altering hit-boxes, heavy physical debuffs).

Specialization B: Cognitive Override (Manipulating enemy aggro, confusing mobs, creating friendly-fire scenarios).

Sub-Class 2: The Anomaly (Focuses on glitch mechanics, void energy, and existing outside the standard rules of combat).

Specialization A: Reality Tearing (High-damage dimensional strikes, unblockable attacks).

Specialization B: Timeline Splintering (Evasion, creating echoes of the player, aggressive positional resets).

Sub-Class 3: The Front-Matter Architect (Focuses on setting the stage of the battle before the primary brawl begins).

Specialization A: Foundation Warding (Heavy shielding, arena-wide buffs, setting defensive perimeters).

Specialization B: Lethal Formatting (Deploying traps, altering the terrain, creating choke points).

Sub-Class 4: The Evolutionary Coder (Focuses on adapting to the enemy's biology and scaling stats mid-fight).

Specialization A: Biomechanical Shift (Stealing enemy traits, converting mechanical damage to organic healing).

Specialization B: Digital Ascension (Sacrificing defense for exponentially scaling attack speed and combo multipliers).

The EPI-Savant: Structural Revision Specialization (Level 1 - 40)
This specialization tree focuses on breaking down the enemy's structural integrity. The gameplay loop rewards players for identifying priority targets, exposing their weaknesses, and using free-flow combos to trigger devastating "Revisions" (combo finishers).

Tier 1: Foundation (Levels 1 - 10)

Level 1: Syntax Strike (Active): Your base light melee attack. Generates 1 Protocol Point upon a successful hit without breaking your combo.

Level 2: Ablative Edits (Passive): Syntax Strike now physically strips away 1% of an enemy’s armor rating per hit. Stacks up to 10% on a single target.

Level 3: Flow-State Analytics (Passive): The grace period before your combo multiplier resets is permanently increased by 0.75 seconds.

Level 4: Vaulting Lexicon (Active): Unlocks the directional vault. Vaulting directly over an enemy’s head applies the Exposed status effect to them for 3 seconds.

Level 5: Structural Rewrite (Active / Finisher): Consumes 5 Protocol Points. A heavy, un-interruptible kinetic slam that shatters Exposed targets, dealing 250% base damage.

Level 6: Momentum Retention (Passive): If Structural Rewrite kills the target, 2 Protocol Points are immediately refunded.

Level 7: Parry Protocol (Active): Standard block is upgraded to a precision parry. Perfectly timing a parry against a melee attack instantly grants 3 Protocol Points.

Level 8: Blunt Trauma (Passive): Increases the stagger duration of perfectly parried enemies by 1.5 seconds.

Level 9: Aerial Extraction (Active): Holding the light attack button launches a staggered enemy into the air, allowing you to transition into an aerial juggle.

Level 10: The Red Pen (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Swipes a wide arc of red energetic code in front of you. Instantly applies Exposed to all enemies hit and interrupts unblockable attacks. 15-second cooldown.

Tier 2: Combo Scaling & Crowd Control (Levels 11 - 20)

Level 11: Kinetic Connectivity (Passive): Aerial juggles now generate 2 Protocol Points per hit instead of 1.

Level 12: Area-of-Effect (AoE) Revisions (Passive): Structural Rewrite now deals 40% of its total damage to all enemies within a 3-meter radius of the primary target.

Level 13: Ground-Swell (Active): Mid-air, press the heavy attack button to dive-bomb the ground. Damage scales directly with your current combo multiplier.

Level 14: Feedback Loop (Passive): Taking damage no longer instantly resets your combo to zero; it now halves your current multiplier instead.

Level 15: Phonetic Resonance (Active / Aura): Toggle ability. Drains 1 Protocol Point per second. While active, every strike emits a low-frequency hum that slows enemy movement speed in an 8-meter radius by 15%.

Level 16: Deflection Matrix (Passive): While Phonetic Resonance is active, incoming projectiles are slowed by 50%, widening the parry window.

Level 17: Grapple Syntax (Active): Unlocks a magnetic energy tether. Pulls lightweight fodder enemies directly to you from up to 15 meters away to sustain combos.

Level 18: Heavy Tether (Passive): Grapple Syntax can now be used on massive Bosses/Titans. Instead of pulling them to you, it rapidly pulls you to them, granting brief invulnerability during travel.

Level 19: Armor Sunder (Passive): Ablative Edits (Level 2) maximum armor reduction stack increased from 10% to 25%.

Level 20: Draft Deletion (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Target one non-boss enemy. If their health is below 30%, instantly execute them, digitizing their body and causing a burst of healing for the player. 30-second cooldown.

Tier 3: Advanced Mechanics & Survivability (Levels 21 - 30)

Level 21: Over-Heal Analytics (Passive): If Draft Deletion is used while you are at full health, the healing is converted into a temporary over-shield.

Level 22: Flawless Flow (Passive): Reaching a 25-hit combo grants a 10% boost to attack speed.

Level 23: Perfect Flow (Passive): Reaching a 50-hit combo grants an additional 15% boost to attack speed and makes your light attacks unblockable by standard shielded mobs.

Level 24: Frame-Trap (Active): Dodge backward precisely as an enemy strikes to leave behind a static structural clone. The enemy will attack the clone, becoming staggered.

Level 25: Explosive Decoy (Passive): The clone created by Frame-Trap now detonates after 2 seconds, dealing moderate kinetic damage.

Level 26: Hard-Coded Health (Passive): Permanently increases maximum health by 15%.

Level 27: Synergy Points (Passive): Protocol Points cap increased from 10 to 20.

Level 28: Dual Rewrite (Active / Finisher): Consumes 10 Protocol Points. Unleashes two rapid-fire Structural Rewrites back-to-back, with the second hit guaranteed to critically strike.

Level 29: Executioner's Grace (Passive): Dual Rewrite now heals you for 5% of your max health if it successfully kills an Exposed target.

Level 30: System Override (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. slamming your fist into the ground, completely suspending all enemies in a 15-meter radius in an anti-gravity stasis for 4 seconds. 60-second cooldown.

Tier 4: Capstones & Mastery (Levels 31 - 40)

Level 31: Stasis Strike (Passive): Hitting enemies suspended by System Override deals double damage but breaks them out of stasis early.

Level 32: Unbroken Chain (Passive): Using System Override no longer pauses your combo timer; it locks it in place, completely preventing it from decaying while the stasis is active.

Level 33: Critical Lexicon (Passive): Base critical hit chance increased by 5%.

Level 34: Weak-Point Targeting (Passive): Critical hit damage increased by 20% against targets with the Exposed status.

Level 35: The Master Protocol (Aura): Consumes 15 Protocol Points to activate. For 10 seconds, all light attacks apply Exposed, and all heavy attacks act as base-level Structural Rewrites.

Level 36: Cooldown Reduction (Passive): Every successful parry reduces the cooldown of all Major Abilities by 1 second.

Level 37: Infinite Grapple (Passive): Grapple Syntax now has zero cooldown and can be used mid-air endlessly to traverse between aerial targets without touching the ground.

Level 38: Kinetic Battery (Passive): Staying airborne for more than 5 seconds grants a stacking damage buff (2% per second) until you touch the floor.

Level 39: Final Revision (Passive): When your health drops below 10%, instantly trigger an automatic System Override centered on you, at no cooldown cost. Can only occur once every 5 minutes.

Level 40: CAPSTONE - EPI-Omniscience (Active / Ultimate): You merge with the battlefield's code. For 15 seconds, you become completely intangible to enemy damage. Your combo multiplier is artificially locked at 100x, and every strike against an enemy permanently reduces their maximum health by 2% for the remainder of the encounter (incredibly effective for burning down Titan-class bosses).

2. The Apex Mutator
Combat Style: Adaptive Brawler

Free-Flow Mechanic: Driven by a volatile evolution mechanic. As the player's combo multiplier increases, this class physically transforms mid-fight, growing monstrous appendages or gaining new elemental properties. Reaching a 50-hit combo might trigger an evolution into a winged state for enhanced aerial juggles. If the combo drops, they revert to their base form, forcing a relentlessly aggressive playstyle.

Class 2 Architecture: The Apex Mutator
The ultimate adaptive brawler, driven by a highly volatile genetic and digital matrix. This class thrives on aggressive momentum, physically evolving into deadlier forms as the combo multiplier climbs.

Sub-Class 1: The Biomech Beast (Focuses on rapid integration of scavenged technology and heavy hydraulic strikes).

Specialization A: Cyber-Strike (High-speed, hyper-mobile limb augmentations).

Specialization B: Scrap-Armor (Defensive plating, transforming into a walking tank).

Sub-Class 2: The Chimera Strand (Focuses on raw organic mutations, splicing different beast traits mid-combat).

Specialization A: Venomous Adaptation (Toxic protrusions, damage-over-time effects, area denial).

Specialization B: Feral Regeneration (Vampiric life-steal, feral speed, and relentless pursuit).

Sub-Class 3: The Data-Code Deviant (Focuses on digital evolution, overwriting physical boundaries, and recursive data consumption).

Specialization A: Recursive Evolution (Fast-tracking distinct evolutionary stages—Alpha, Beta, Omega).

Specialization B: Corrupted File (Inflicting glitch mechanics, altering enemy behavior, and timeline stuttering).

Sub-Class 4: The Primal Catalyst (Focuses on awakening ancient, raw, towering beast forms).

Specialization A: Earth-Shaker (Heavy Area-of-Effect, tectonic shockwaves, and crowd disruption).

Specialization B: Apex Predator (Single-target burst damage, isolation tactics, and armor piercing).

The Data-Code Deviant: Recursive Evolution Specialization (Level 1 - 40)
This specialization tree revolves around a distinct, tiered evolutionary ladder. By sustaining an unbroken flow-state, the player forces their character to digitally "digivolve" into larger, more devastating forms mid-fight. Dropping the combo devolves the player, demanding a relentless, hyper-aggressive playstyle.

Tier 1: Foundation & The Alpha Stage (Levels 1 - 10)

Level 1: Data-Rend (Active): Your base light melee attack. Generates 1 Evolution Point (EP) upon a successful hit.

Level 2: Alpha Trigger (Passive): Reaching a 10-hit combo instantly evolves you into your Alpha Form, increasing movement speed by 15% and slightly altering your physical silhouette with glowing, digital geometry.

Level 3: Feral Glide (Active): Unlocks a frictionless, digital air-dash to instantly close gaps between isolated targets and maintain your combo.

Level 4: Alpha Striker (Passive): While in Alpha Form, Data-Rend hits twice per input, effectively doubling EP generation.

Level 5: DNA Siphon (Active / Finisher): Consumes 5 EP. A vicious, latching bite that drains data from the target, healing you for 5% of your maximum health.

Level 6: Digitize Fodder (Passive): Killing an enemy instantly grants 2 EP and pauses the combo decay timer for 1 second.

Level 7: Reactive Carapace (Active): Standard block is upgraded to a parry. Perfectly timing a parry briefly hardens your digital skin, staggering the attacker and generating 3 EP.

Level 8: Structural Integrity (Passive): If you take damage, you now drop one Evolution Stage instead of instantly reverting all the way to your Base Form.

Level 9: Launch Pad (Active): Holding the heavy attack button executes a massive, launching uppercut, allowing you to transition seamlessly into an aerial juggle.

Level 10: Beta Trigger (Passive): Reaching a 25-hit combo evolves you into your Beta Form. You grow noticeably larger; light attacks gain a 2-meter Area-of-Effect (AoE) shockwave.

Tier 2: Combo Scaling & Mid-Tier Evolution (Levels 11 - 20)

Level 11: Beta-Sweep (Active): While in Beta Form, holding the light attack button performs a massive, 360-degree tail spin that knocks down surrounding fodder enemies.

Level 12: Kinetic Battery (Passive): As long as you are actively moving (sprinting, vaulting, or attacking), EP generation is increased by 20%.

Level 13: Aerial Pounce (Active): Mid-air, press the heavy attack button to dive-bomb an enemy. Damage scales with your current combo multiplier.

Level 14: Hard-Coded Biology (Passive): Permanently increases maximum health by 15%.

Level 15: Assimilation Roar (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Unleashes a digitized roar. Fears low-level fodder for 3 seconds and taunts larger enemies to attack you directly. 20-second cooldown.

Level 16: Data-Spike (Passive): Beta-Sweep now afflicts hit enemies with Corrupted Code, causing them to take 5% of their maximum health as damage over 4 seconds.

Level 17: Vaulting Mutation (Active): Unlocks directional vault. Vaulting over an enemy briefly steals their defense stat, adding it to your own for 3 seconds.

Level 18: Symbiotic Link (Passive): In multiplayer, if an ally executes a combo finisher within 10 meters of you, you are instantly granted 2 EP.

Level 19: Armor Sunder (Passive): DNA Siphon (Level 5) now permanently shreds 15% of the target's armor upon a successful hit.

Level 20: Omega Threshold (Passive): Reaching a 50-hit combo evolves you into your Omega Form. You become a massive, bipedal beast of pure data. All standard light attacks become completely unblockable by normal enemies.

Tier 3: Advanced Mechanics & Survivability (Levels 21 - 30)

Level 21: Omega Cleave (Active): Replaces Data-Rend in Omega Form. A massive, sweeping claw attack that hits all enemies in a frontal cone, dealing 150% base damage.

Level 22: Rapid Regression (Passive): If your combo timer runs out while in Beta or Omega Form, you explode with digital energy, dealing damage to all nearby enemies proportional to the lost combo size.

Level 23: Perfect Flow (Passive): Taking a hit in Omega Form no longer immediately degrades your form. Instead, it consumes 15 hits from your combo meter as a "shield."

Level 24: Frame-Trap (Active): Dodge backward precisely as an enemy strikes to leave behind a hollow, molted shell of your current evolutionary stage. The enemy will attack the shell and become staggered.

Level 25: Molted Detonation (Passive): The shell created by Frame-Trap detonates after 2 seconds, knocking enemies into the air.

Level 26: Base Code Optimization (Passive): Permanently increases base damage of all attacks by 10%.

Level 27: Evolution Cap (Passive): Maximum EP storage capacity is increased from 10 to 20.

Level 28: Dual Siphon (Active / Finisher): Consumes 10 EP. DNA Siphon now strikes twice rapidly, doubling the healing and armor-shredding effects.

Level 29: Feral Grace (Passive): Dodge and vault distance increased by 20%.

Level 30: The Anomaly Virus (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Inject a single target with a highly volatile digital virus. If they die within 5 seconds, they explode into 5 homing projectiles that track other enemies. 45-second cooldown.

Tier 4: Capstones & Mastery (Levels 31 - 40)

Level 31: Viral Spread (Passive): The homing projectiles from The Anomaly Virus apply the Corrupted Code damage-over-time effect to secondary targets.

Level 32: Unbroken Chain (Passive): Being stunned or knocked down no longer resets your combo multiplier; it merely pauses the decay timer until you recover.

Level 33: Critical Mutation (Passive): Base critical hit chance increased by 5%.

Level 34: Weak-Point Targeting (Passive): Critical hit damage increased by 20% when attacking targets inflicted with Corrupted Code.

Level 35: The Master Form (Aura): Consumes 15 EP to activate. For 10 seconds, you are locked into Omega Form regardless of your current combo multiplier.

Level 36: Cooldown Reduction (Passive): Every successful parry reduces the cooldown of Assimilation Roar and The Anomaly Virus by 1 second.

Level 37: Infinite Vault (Passive): You can now vault mid-air indefinitely, allowing you to bounce from enemy head to enemy head without ever touching the ground.

Level 38: Kinetic Battery II (Passive): Staying airborne for more than 5 seconds grants a stacking damage buff (2% per second) until you touch the floor.

Level 39: Forced Ascension (Passive): When your health drops below 10%, you instantly trigger an automatic evolution into Omega Form and heal for 25% of your max health. Can only occur once every 5 minutes.

Level 40: CAPSTONE - Apex Ascendancy (Active / Ultimate): Consumes a 100x combo multiplier to activate. You digitize into a screen-clearing, primeval avatar of pure corrupted code for 15 seconds. You are entirely invincible, and every single strike causes a cascading chain reaction of digital explosions, essentially turning the entire arena into an active hazard for your enemies.

3. The Resonant
Combat Style: Rhythm-Based Area of Effect

Free-Flow Mechanic: A highly kinetic class that treats combat like a heavy bass drop. They attack using low-frequency shockwaves and sweeping, flow-arts movement. Every successful timed counter unleashes a resonant blast that stuns surrounding enemies. Their combat loops are entirely rhythm-dependent, rewarding perfect timing to the "beat" of the fight with massive area-of-effect damage.

Class 3 Architecture: The Resonant
The kinetic master of the battlefield, treating combat as a heavy bass performance. This class relies on rhythmic strikes, flow-arts movement, and low-frequency area denial to control the tempo of the fight.

Sub-Class 1: The Sub-Bass Architect (Focuses on heavy, low-frequency shockwaves, ground control, and massive area-of-effect stuns).

Specialization A: Low-Frequency Disruption (Tectonic slams, shattering enemy shields, staggering giant bosses).

Specialization B: Kinetic Amplification (Storing kinetic energy from hits and releasing it as concentrated sonic blasts).

Sub-Class 2: The Tempo-Weaver (Focuses on speeding up or slowing down the flow of combat through rhythmic manipulation).

Specialization A: Accelerando (Exponentially increasing attack speed and dash distance as the combo climbs).

Specialization B: Halftime Stasis (Slowing enemy attack animations and projecting localized time-dilation fields).

Sub-Class 3: The Sonic Vanguard (Focuses on defensive sound-barriers, projectile deflection, and holding the frontline).

Specialization A: Acoustic Shielding (Creating walls of solid sound to absorb heavy blows).

Specialization B: Reverb Deflection (Bouncing enemy projectiles back with multiplied force).

Sub-Class 4: The Wakaan Mystic (Focuses on mind-altering frequencies, ethereal flow-arts, and confusing enemy AI).

Specialization A: Psychoacoustic Illusion (Creating auditory clones, manipulating aggro, and disorienting hordes).

Specialization B: Ethereal Resonance (Phasing through solid matter during the "drop," applying debuffs via soundwaves).

The Sub-Bass Architect: Low-Frequency Disruption Specialization (Level 1 - 40)
This specialization tree revolves around the concept of the "Drop." The player builds up acoustic pressure by striking to a rhythm, ultimately unleashing massive, un-interruptible shockwaves that clear the arena and juggle enemies using pure sound.

Tier 1: Foundation & The Beat (Levels 1 - 10)

Level 1: Metric Strike (Active): Your base light melee attack. Generates 1 Decibel (dB) charge per hit.

Level 2: Perfect Pitch (Passive): Hitting an enemy exactly on the "beat" (a visual/audio pulse in the combo meter) generates 2 dB charges and slightly increases the damage of the strike.

Level 3: Flow-Arts Evasion (Active): Unlocks a rhythmic, spinning dodge. Dodging on the beat perfectly preserves your combo multiplier and grants a brief window of invulnerability.

Level 4: Sub-Woofer Slam (Active / Finisher): Consumes 10 dB. A heavy, ground-pounding kinetic strike that creates a 3-meter shockwave, knocking down all lightweight fodder.

Level 5: Resonance Tuning (Passive): Enemies hit by Sub-Woofer Slam have their physical armor reduced by 10% for 5 seconds.

Level 6: Acoustic Counter (Active): Replaces standard block. Parrying an attack releases a sharp burst of feedback, staggering the attacker and instantly generating 5 dB.

Level 7: The Build-Up (Passive): As your combo multiplier climbs above 15, your light attacks passively emit a low hum that slows the movement speed of enemies within 2 meters.

Level 8: Aerial Kick-Drum (Active): Holding the heavy attack button mid-air causes you to crash down with immense force, launching nearby staggered enemies into the air.

Level 9: Extended Range (Passive): The shockwave radius of Sub-Woofer Slam is increased from 3 meters to 5 meters.

Level 10: The Bass Drop (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. You channel raw low-frequency energy into a devastating directional cone. Shatters enemy shields and completely deafens/disorients surviving targets for 4 seconds. 20-second cooldown.

Tier 2: Combo Scaling & Shockwave Mastery (Levels 11 - 20)

Level 11: Kinetic Feedback (Passive): Hitting enemies who are actively disoriented by The Bass Drop generates double dB charges.

Level 12: Tremor Vault (Active): Unlocks directional vault. Vaulting over a large enemy plants a "sonic charge" on their back that detonates after 2 seconds, dealing localized burst damage.

Level 13: Ground-Loop (Passive): If Sub-Woofer Slam hits more than 3 enemies at once, 50% of the dB cost is instantly refunded.

Level 14: Structural Resonance (Passive): Permanently increases maximum health by 10% and base physical defense by 5%.

Level 15: Heavy Wubs (Active / Aura): Toggle ability. Constantly drains 2 dB per second. While active, every step you take emits a micro-tremor that interrupts enemy ranged attack animations.

Level 16: Defibrillator (Passive): Executing a perfect Acoustic Counter heals you for 3% of your maximum health.

Level 17: Wall of Sound (Active): Pressing the light and heavy attack buttons simultaneously projects a stationary wall of hard-light and sound that absorbs incoming projectiles for 4 seconds.

Level 18: Reverb (Passive): Enemies that physically strike the Wall of Sound are knocked backward and take minor sonic damage.

Level 19: Deep Frequency (Passive): Resonance Tuning (Level 5) armor reduction is increased from 10% to 25%.

Level 20: Tectonic Shift (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. You slam the ground, causing the very earth beneath you to ripple like water. All enemies within 10 meters are violently thrown into the air, allowing you to easily begin an aerial juggle on any target. 35-second cooldown.

Tier 3: Advanced Mechanics & Survivability (Levels 21 - 30)

Level 21: Anti-Gravity Juggles (Passive): Enemies launched by Tectonic Shift fall 50% slower, giving you a massive window to execute complex mid-air combos.

Level 22: Unbreakable Rhythm (Passive): Reaching a 30-hit combo makes you completely immune to being staggered by light enemy attacks.

Level 23: Perfect Flow (Passive): Reaching a 60-hit combo adds a secondary echo to all of your light attacks, effectively causing every strike to hit twice.

Level 24: Frame-Trap (Active): Dodge backward precisely as an enemy strikes to leave behind a concentrated orb of screeching feedback. The enemy attacks the orb, triggering a flashbang effect.

Level 25: Deafening Echo (Passive): The flashbang from Frame-Trap now heavily reduces the attack damage of blinded enemies by 30% for 5 seconds.

Level 26: Sub-Harmonic Healing (Passive): Permanently increases all incoming healing effectiveness by 15%.

Level 27: Maximum Volume (Passive): Maximum dB storage capacity is increased from 20 to 40.

Level 28: Dual-Woofer Slam (Active / Finisher): Consumes 20 dB. Executes two back-to-back Sub-Woofer Slams. The second slam has double the radius and automatically critically strikes.

Level 29: Rhythmic Grace (Passive): Dodge and vault animations are 15% faster and travel 15% further.

Level 30: The Soundscape (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. You deploy a localized arena-wide aura. For 10 seconds, all enemies moving inside the Soundscape move in slow-motion, while you and your allies move at normal speed. 50-second cooldown.

Tier 4: Capstones & Mastery (Levels 31 - 40)

Level 31: Lethal Acoustics (Passive): Enemies caught inside The Soundscape take 15% more damage from all sources.

Level 32: Unbroken Chain (Passive): Taking a heavy hit no longer resets your combo multiplier; it merely reduces it by 10 hits and pushes you backward.

Level 33: Critical Frequency (Passive): Base critical hit chance increased by 5%.

Level 34: Weak-Point Targeting (Passive): Critical hit damage increased by 20% against deafened or disoriented targets.

Level 35: The Master Mixer (Aura): Consumes 30 dB to activate. For 10 seconds, every single attack you land automatically registers as being perfectly on the "beat," granting maximum damage and dB generation regardless of your actual timing.

Level 36: Cooldown Reduction (Passive): Every successful Acoustic Counter reduces the cooldown of Tectonic Shift and The Soundscape by 1.5 seconds.

Level 37: Infinite Vault (Passive): You can now vault mid-air indefinitely by bouncing off the solid soundwaves you create under your own feet.

Level 38: Kinetic Battery (Passive): Staying airborne for more than 5 seconds grants a stacking damage buff (2% per second) until you touch the floor.

Level 39: Emergency Override (Passive): When your health drops below 10%, you instantly trigger an automatic Tectonic Shift centered on yourself, throwing all threats away from you. Can only occur once every 5 minutes.

Level 40: CAPSTONE - The Festival Headliner (Active / Ultimate): Consumes a 100x combo multiplier to activate. You float above the arena, transforming into a conduit of pure, destructive frequency. For 12 seconds, you cannot be damaged, and you project continuous, rippling shockwaves across the entire battlefield that deal massive damage, permanently shatter all enemy armor plating, and juggle every non-boss enemy in a state of suspended animation.

4. The Packmaster
Combat Style: Tag-Team / Grappler

Free-Flow Mechanic: Fights seamlessly alongside a heavily armored, aggressive canine companion. The core loop revolves around marking priority targets for the companion to latch onto with a heavy-chewing bite. While the enemy is pinned and their attacks are disrupted, the player can vault off their companion's back to launch into devastating aerial combos on surrounding foes.

Class 4 Architecture: The Packmaster
The ultimate tag-team brawler. This class never fights alone, utilizing an aggressive, heavily augmented canine companion to lock down priority targets, break enemy formations, and extend free-flow combos across massive arenas.

Sub-Class 1: The Alpha-Handler (Focuses on direct commands, joint-strikes, and using the companion for extreme crowd control).

Specialization A: Heavy-Chewer Lockdown (Pinning high-threat targets, shattering armor, and sustained damage-over-time).

Specialization B: Coordinated Assault (Rapidly swapping aggro, multiplying combo points through tag-team finishers).

Sub-Class 2: The Feral Vanguard (Focuses on the player adopting the beast's traits, fighting side-by-side in a flurry of claws and blades).

Specialization A: Blood-Scent (Tracking wounded enemies, increasing critical strike chance).

Specialization B: Pack Mentality (Sharing health pools, mirroring attacks, and defensive buffs).

Sub-Class 3: The Outward Hunter (Focuses on maximizing the distance between player and companion to control massive zones).

Specialization A: Flanking Maneuvers (Companion attacks from the rear, bypassing standard shields).

Specialization B: Territorial Divide (Drawing lines of control, intercepting charging fodder).

Sub-Class 4: The Hound-Rider (Focuses on utilizing the massive companion as a mount for heavy kinetic traversal and trampling).

Specialization A: The Stampede (Unstoppable momentum, plowing through crowds).

Specialization B: Mounted Artillery (Firing from atop the beast while it automatically evades).

The Alpha-Handler: Heavy-Chewer Lockdown Specialization (Level 1 - 40)
This specialization tree turns your canine companion into an unbreakable vise. The gameplay loop involves directing the hound to latch onto the most dangerous enemy on the field, entirely removing them from the fight while you safely build your free-flow combo on the surrounding fodder.

Tier 1: Foundation & The Hunt (Levels 1 - 10)

Level 1: Twin-Strike (Active): Your base light melee attack. Generates 1 Command Point (CP) upon a successful hit.

Level 2: The Latch (Active): Tap the command button to send the companion to bite and hold your current target. The enemy is completely immobilized for 3 seconds but takes reduced damage from your strikes while pinned.

Level 3: Vaulting Assist (Active): Unlocks directional vault. If you vault toward an enemy currently pinned by The Latch, you spring off the companion's back, launching yourself into an aerial combo while instantly generating 2 CP.

Level 4: K-0NG Reinforced Jaws (Passive): The companion’s teeth are upgraded with ultra-durable synthetics. The Latch now permanently shreds 15% of an enemy's base armor when the pin ends.

Level 5: Heel & Heel-Strike (Active / Finisher): Consumes 5 CP. Recall the companion instantly to your side. As it returns, it wildly bashes through any enemies in its path, briefly staggering them.

Level 6: Momentum Share (Passive): If the companion kills an enemy while acting autonomously, your combo multiplier increases by 2.

Level 7: Tag-Team Parry (Active): Standard block is upgraded. If you perfectly parry an incoming attack, the companion instantly lunges at the attacker, interrupting their next animation.

Level 8: The Shake (Passive): While The Latch is active, the companion violently shakes the target, causing 5% of their max health as physical damage over the 3-second duration.

Level 9: Launching Bite (Active): Command the companion to perform a heavy uppercut bite, throwing an isolated enemy into the air for you to juggle.

Level 10: Sic 'Em (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. The companion goes into a frenzy, rapidly teleporting/dashing between up to 5 different targets, applying a 1-second Latch to each and grouping them tightly together. 20-second cooldown.

Tier 2: Combo Scaling & Crowd Control (Levels 11 - 20)

Level 11: Kinetic Bond (Passive): Striking an enemy that is currently afflicted by The Latch generates double CP.

Level 12: Meat-Shield (Active): If an unblockable projectile is about to hit you, consuming 3 CP causes the companion to leap in front of you, absorbing the blow completely without taking damage.

Level 13: Ground-Pound Intercept (Passive): If you are knocked down, the companion automatically unleashes a 3-meter AoE shockwave to push enemies back while you recover.

Level 14: Structural Hardiness (Passive): Permanently increases your maximum health and the companion's damage resistance by 15%.

Level 15: Ferocious Growl (Active / Aura): Toggle ability. Drains 1 CP per second. The companion emits a terrifying low-frequency growl. All fodder-class enemies within 8 meters are too intimidated to initiate attacks.

Level 16: Opportunistic Strikes (Passive): While Ferocious Growl is active, your critical hit chance against intimidated enemies increases by 10%.

Level 17: Drag to Hell (Active): Command the companion to latch onto an enemy and drag them forcefully across the arena directly to your feet, knocking over any enemies in the way like bowling pins.

Level 18: Unyielding Grip (Passive): The duration of The Latch is increased from 3 seconds to 5 seconds on Boss and Titan-class enemies.

Level 19: Deep Tissue Tear (Passive): K-0NG Reinforced Jaws (Level 4) armor reduction is increased from 15% to 30%.

Level 20: Alpha's Command (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. You and the companion target the same enemy. You perform a synchronized, high-damage flurry of attacks. If this ability kills the target, it resets the cooldown of all your Major Abilities. 40-second cooldown.

Tier 3: Advanced Mechanics & Survivability (Levels 21 - 30)

Level 21: Over-Heal Analytics (Passive): If Alpha's Command successfully kills a target, both you and the companion are healed for 15% of your max health.

Level 22: Flawless Pack (Passive): Reaching a 25-hit combo causes the companion's standard attacks to emit shockwaves, damaging adjacent enemies.

Level 23: Perfect Pack (Passive): Reaching a 50-hit combo infuses the companion with kinetic energy. Their Latch now completely ignores enemy shielding.

Level 24: Frame-Trap Bait (Active): Dodge backward precisely as an enemy strikes. The companion instantly swaps positions with you, taking the hit and retaliating with a guaranteed critical strike.

Level 25: Retaliation Force (Passive): The guaranteed critical strike from Frame-Trap Bait knocks the enemy into a suspended aerial juggle state.

Level 26: Bestial Vigor (Passive): Permanently increases base movement speed and dodge distance by 10%.

Level 27: Maximum Command (Passive): CP storage capacity is increased from 10 to 20.

Level 28: Dual-Latch (Active / Finisher): Consumes 10 CP. The companion splits into two hard-light visual echoes of itself, capable of locking down two separate heavy targets simultaneously.

Level 29: Shared Senses (Passive): You gain complete immunity to blindness and disorientation status effects.

Level 30: The Den (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. You slam the ground, creating a 15-meter circular perimeter of hard-light thorns. Enemies cannot enter or exit the perimeter for 8 seconds, trapping you, the companion, and your prey in a cage match. 50-second cooldown.

Tier 4: Capstones & Mastery (Levels 31 - 40)

Level 31: Cornered Beasts (Passive): While inside The Den, you and your companion deal 20% increased damage.

Level 32: Unbroken Chain (Passive): Being staggered by an enemy no longer resets your combo timer as long as the companion is actively dealing damage to any target on the field.

Level 33: Critical Synergy (Passive): Base critical hit damage increased by 15% for both you and the companion.

Level 34: Executioner's Mark (Passive): If an enemy drops below 10% health, the companion will automatically abandon its current task to instantly execute them (does not work on Titans/Bosses).

Level 35: The Master Handler (Aura): Consumes 15 CP to activate. For 10 seconds, every time you strike an enemy, the companion instantly teleports to that enemy and strikes them simultaneously, effectively doubling your hit count and damage output.

Level 36: Cooldown Reduction (Passive): Every successful Tag-Team Parry reduces the cooldown of Sic 'Em and The Den by 1.5 seconds.

Level 37: Infinite Vault Assist (Passive): You can now bounce off the companion's back mid-air indefinitely, allowing you to juggle enemies in the sky without touching the ground as the companion maneuvers beneath you to catch your fall.

Level 38: Kinetic Battery (Passive): Staying airborne for more than 5 seconds grants a stacking damage buff (2% per second) until you touch the floor.

Level 39: Guardian Angel (Passive): When your health drops below 5%, the companion forcefully grabs you and bounds 30 meters away from the danger zone, granting you a temporary 50% health shield. Can only occur once every 5 minutes.

Level 40: CAPSTONE - Release the Hound (Active / Ultimate): Consumes a 100x combo multiplier to activate. You take a knee and direct all your kinetic energy into the companion. For 15 seconds, the companion grows to the size of a Titan and enters an autonomous, uncontrollable rampage. It becomes entirely invincible, its jaws crush all enemy armor ratings to zero, and every step it takes causes localized earthquakes that continuously juggle all mobs in the arena.

5. The Orbital Striker
Combat Style: Aerial Specialist / Mobility

Free-Flow Mechanic: Equipped with experimental zero-gravity thrusters, this class mimics the weightlessness of space travel. They excel at launching enemies into the air and keeping them suspended indefinitely. Their dodges are frictionless glides, allowing them to cross massive arenas instantly and juggle multiple enemies without ever touching the floor.

Class 5 Architecture: The Orbital Striker
Equipped with experimental zero-gravity thrusters, this class abandons the ground entirely. They excel at launching enemies into the stratosphere and keeping them suspended indefinitely, treating the air as their primary domain.

Sub-Class 1: The Zero-G Brawler (Focuses on launching enemies and fighting exclusively in mid-air juggles).

Specialization A: Atmospheric Juggle (Infinite air combos, frictionless repositioning, keeping enemies suspended).

Specialization B: Meteor Crash (Converting extreme aerial height and hang-time into devastating, screen-clearing ground slams).

Sub-Class 2: The Thruster-Junkie (Focuses on extreme horizontal mobility and hit-and-run momentum).

Specialization A: Frictionless Dash (Gliding across arenas instantly, speed-scaling damage).

Specialization B: Exhaust Burn (Leaving lethal trails of superheated plasma, close-quarters thrust-kicks).

Sub-Class 3: The Grav-Architect (Focuses on controlling the localized gravity of the arena itself).

Specialization A: Singularity Tether (Pulling scattered enemies into a single floating cluster).

Specialization B: Repulsion Matrix (Violently pushing enemies away, creating localized zero-G zones for allies).

Sub-Class 4: The Orbital Bombardment (Focuses on designating targets for heavy off-screen artillery).

Specialization A: Satellite Painting (Marking priority targets for delayed, massive energy beams).

Specialization B: Kinetic Rods (Calling down heavy physical pillars that alter the arena's terrain and create stepping stones).

The Zero-G Brawler: Atmospheric Juggle Specialization (Level 1 - 40)
This tree completely flips standard combat design. The ground is lava; your goal is to launch enemies and yourself into the air and never come back down. Your damage, defense, and combo multiplier scale exponentially the longer your feet are off the floor.

Tier 1: Foundation & Liftoff (Levels 1 - 10)

Level 1: Thruster-Strike (Active): Your base light melee attack. Generates 1 Altitude (ALT) Charge upon a successful hit.

Level 2: Anti-Grav Uppercut (Passive): Holding the light attack button physically reverses the gravity on a single enemy, instantly launching them 10 meters into the air alongside you.

Level 3: Hover-Dash (Active): Unlocks a frictionless mid-air dodge. Dodging laterally in the air preserves your altitude and maintains your combo multiplier.

Level 4: Stratosphere Slam (Active / Finisher): Consumes 5 ALT Charges. A brutal mid-air axe kick that sends a juggled enemy rocketing back into the floor, creating a kinetic shockwave on impact.

Level 5: Hang-Time Analytics (Passive): For every consecutive second you remain airborne, your light attack damage increases by 2% (caps at 20%).

Level 6: Thruster Parry (Active): Standard block is upgraded. Perfectly timing a block mid-air fires a short burst from your thrusters, staggering the enemy and resetting your mid-air jump count.

Level 7: Aerodynamic Flow (Passive): Your combo decay timer pauses completely as long as you are actively performing a mid-air dash or vault.

Level 8: Tractor Grapple (Active): Fire a magnetic tether at an enemy on the ground, instantly ripping them up into the air to join your current juggle.

Level 9: Helium Core (Passive): Your base falling speed is permanently reduced by 50%, giving you wider windows to connect aerial combos.

Level 10: The Grav-Lift (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Deploy a localized anti-gravity well on the floor beneath you. All enemies that step into the 5-meter radius are slowly floated into the air, completely defenseless. 20-second cooldown.

Tier 2: Combo Scaling & Aerial Dominance (Levels 11 - 20)

Level 11: Kinetic Transfer (Passive): Striking an enemy caught inside The Grav-Lift generates double ALT Charges.

Level 12: Vaulting Ascent (Active): Unlocks directional vault. Vaulting off an enemy's head propels you even higher into the air and guarantees your next strike will be a critical hit.

Level 13: Mid-Air Intercept (Passive): If an enemy attempts to leap at you while you are airborne, your next Thruster-Strike will automatically teleport you to them, countering their attack.

Level 14: Structural Lightweight (Passive): Permanently increases maximum stamina/energy by 20% and base movement speed by 10%.

Level 15: Vacuum Aura (Active / Aura): Toggle ability. Drains 1 ALT Charge per second. You emit a localized vacuum field that slowly pulls floating enemies closer to your melee range, preventing them from drifting away.

Level 16: Deflection Rotors (Passive): While Vacuum Aura is active, your spinning aerial attacks automatically deflect small-arms projectiles back at the ground.

Level 17: Ground-Zero Pull (Active): Command your thrusters to reverse, violently yanking you from maximum altitude directly to the floor to stomp a priority target, instantly grounding you but dealing massive burst damage.

Level 18: Altitude Sickness (Passive): Enemies kept in the air for more than 4 seconds begin to suffer from Vertigo, reducing their physical defense by 15%.

Level 19: Atmospheric Entry (Passive): Stratosphere Slam (Level 4) now applies a burning damage-over-time effect to the target upon hitting the ground due to reentry friction.

Level 20: Orbital Singularity (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Throw a miniature black hole into the center of the arena suspended 15 meters in the air. It rapidly sucks all lightweight and medium enemies off the floor, clumping them together in the sky for massive AoE combos. 40-second cooldown.

Tier 3: Advanced Mechanics & Survivability (Levels 21 - 30)

Level 21: Event Horizon (Passive): Enemies trapped in the Orbital Singularity take 10% more damage from all aerial attacks.

Level 22: Flawless Flight (Passive): Reaching a 25-hit combo while airborne grants you a temporary over-shield that absorbs one hit without breaking your combo or knocking you down.

Level 23: Perfect Flight (Passive): Reaching a 50-hit combo allows your Tractor Grapple (Level 8) to target up to three enemies simultaneously, pulling an entire squad into the sky.

Level 24: Frame-Trap Afterburner (Active): Dodge backward mid-air precisely as an enemy strikes to leave behind a superheated exhaust cloud. The enemy strikes the cloud and is temporarily blinded and burned.

Level 25: Thermal Updraft (Passive): The superheated cloud from Frame-Trap Afterburner creates an updraft. Passing through it instantly restores your mid-air jump and dash counters.

Level 26: Gyroscopic Stabilizers (Passive): You gain complete immunity to being knocked down or grounded by heavy enemy attacks; you are instead just pushed backward in the air.

Level 27: Maximum Fuel (Passive): ALT Charge storage capacity is increased from 10 to 20.

Level 28: Dual Stratosphere (Active / Finisher): Consumes 10 ALT Charges. Grab two floating enemies simultaneously and slam them both into the ground. The resulting shockwave is doubled in size.

Level 29: Zero-G Grace (Passive): Mid-air dodge distance and vaulting range are permanently increased by 25%.

Level 30: The Exosphere Stasis (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. You snap your fingers, instantly freezing every currently airborne enemy in absolute time-stasis for 6 seconds. They cannot fall, move, or attack. 50-second cooldown.

Tier 4: Capstones & Mastery (Levels 31 - 40)

Level 31: Stasis Shatter (Passive): Hitting enemies trapped in The Exosphere Stasis builds up stored kinetic energy. When the stasis breaks, they take all the accumulated combo damage at once in a massive burst.

Level 32: Unbroken Orbit (Passive): Touching the ground no longer resets your combo multiplier; it merely halves it, giving you a chance to launch back into the air.

Level 33: Critical Altitude (Passive): Base critical hit chance increased by 10% while you are at least 5 meters off the ground.

Level 34: Weak-Point Targeting (Passive): Critical hit damage increased by 20% against enemies suffering from Vertigo.

Level 35: The Master Aviator (Aura): Consumes 15 ALT Charges to activate. For 10 seconds, your thrusters enter overdrive. You can fly freely in three dimensions (like standard swimming controls) without needing to combo enemies to stay afloat.

Level 36: Cooldown Reduction (Passive): Every successful Thruster Parry reduces the cooldown of Orbital Singularity and The Exosphere Stasis by 1.5 seconds.

Level 37: Infinite Grapple (Passive): Tractor Grapple now has zero cooldown and can be woven infinitely between light attacks to constantly feed new targets into your aerial blender.

Level 38: Kinetic Battery (Passive): Hang-Time Analytics (Level 5) damage cap is completely removed. Your damage now scales infinitely by 2% for every second you remain airborne until the combat encounter ends.

Level 39: Emergency Thrusters (Passive): When your health drops below 10%, your thrusters automatically detonate, launching you 50 meters into the air and away from danger while instantly fully recharging your shields. Can only occur once every 5 minutes.

Level 40: CAPSTONE - The Rod of God (Active / Ultimate): Consumes a 100x combo multiplier to activate. You launch yourself so high you briefly exit the arena's rendering bounds. You then select a target area on the ground and crash down like a kinetic meteor at Mach 5. The impact deals catastrophic, arena-wide damage, instantly vaporizes all non-boss enemies, and applies a permanent anti-gravity debuff to surviving Bosses, forcing them to float helplessly for the next 10 seconds.

6. The Scrap-Tek
Combat Style: Biomechanical / Harasser

Free-Flow Mechanic: Relies on scavenged, automated technology and hydraulic limbs. They can seamlessly deploy temporary, hovering turrets or drop shock-traps mid-combo without breaking their attack animation. Their primary traversal tool is a magnetic grapple that rips fleeing enemies back into the center of the melee fray.

Class 6 Architecture: The Scrap-Tek
The ultimate battlefield improviser. Relying on automated technology, hydraulic augments, and scavenged weaponry, this class seamlessly weaves deployable traps and turrets into their free-flow melee combos.

Sub-Class 1: The Scavenger (Focuses on magnetic grapples, recycling enemy armor, and turning battlefield debris into kinetic weapons).

Specialization A: Magnetic Harvester (Ripping armor off foes, chaining enemies together with tethers).

Specialization B: Shrapnel Storm (Explosive debris, area-denial caltrops, and bleed effects).

Sub-Class 2: The Field-Mechanic (Focuses on deploying autonomous drones and turrets that maintain the combo meter while the player repositions).

Specialization A: Sentry Defense (Stationary heavy-fire turrets, creating fortified zones).

Specialization B: Hunter-Killer Drones (Mobile drones that track targets, laser-targeting combos).

Sub-Class 3: The Shock-Jockey (Focuses on high-voltage electrical traps, stunning crowds, and chain-lightning finishers).

Specialization A: Static Grid (Electrifying the floor, localized stun zones).

Specialization B: Overcharge (Sacrificing health/shields for massive bursts of electrical speed and damage).

Sub-Class 4: The Exo-Brawler (Focuses on raw, hydraulic-powered physical strikes and heavy mechanical mobility).

Specialization A: Piston-Strike (Slow, unblockable punches that launch heavy enemies).

Specialization B: Hydraulic Leap (Massive vertical bounds, crashing down to shatter enemy formations).

The Scavenger: Magnetic Harvester Specialization (Level 1 - 40)
This specialization tree is all about battlefield control through magnetism. The player acts as the center of a chaotic orbit, constantly ripping enemies toward them, stripping their armor for personal shielding, and weaponizing the very trash left behind by the brawl.

Tier 1: Foundation & The Magnet (Levels 1 - 10)

Level 1: Ratchet-Strike (Active): Your base light melee attack. Generates 1 Scrap Charge upon a successful hit.

Level 2: Magnetic Tether (Active): Tap the heavy attack button to fire a wrist-mounted magnet. Pulls lightweight fodder instantly to your fist, generating 2 Scrap Charges.

Level 3: Vaulting Caltrops (Active): Unlocks directional vault. Vaulting over an enemy drops a cluster of jagged scrap on their head, staggering them and heavily reducing their movement speed.

Level 4: Hydraulic Piston (Active / Finisher): Consumes 5 Scrap Charges. A devastating, point-blank mechanical punch that shatters enemy shields and knocks the target backward like a projectile.

Level 5: Salvage Protocol (Passive): Whenever an enemy is killed, they drop a physical piece of scrap on the floor. Running over it automatically absorbs it, granting 1 Scrap Charge.

Level 6: Repulsor Parry (Active): Standard block is upgraded. Perfectly parrying an attack reverses the polarity of your gauntlets, repelling the attacker and disarming them of their weapon for 3 seconds.

Level 7: Recycled Armor (Passive): For every 5 Scrap Charges you hold, you passively gain a 2% damage reduction buff (max 10%).

Level 8: Aerial Ripcord (Active): Holding the heavy attack button fires the Magnetic Tether into the air, launching you toward a flying or launched enemy to begin an aerial juggle.

Level 9: Jagged Edges (Passive): Enemies hit by Hydraulic Piston suffer from Tetanus, taking minor physical damage over time for 5 seconds.

Level 10: The Junkyard Turret (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Instantly construct a temporary, automated turret out of your current Scrap Charges. It fires rapidly at your locked-on target for 8 seconds, building your combo multiplier autonomously. 20-second cooldown.

Tier 2: Combo Scaling & Battlefield Control (Levels 11 - 20)

Level 11: Coordinated Fire (Passive): Striking the same enemy that your Junkyard Turret is currently shooting generates double Scrap Charges.

Level 12: Tether Whip (Active): If you use Magnetic Tether on a heavy Titan/Boss, you cannot pull them. Instead, you instantly pull yourself to them, closing the gap for an immediate flurry of strikes.

Level 13: Ground-Slam Magnetics (Passive): Mid-air heavy attacks now emit a magnetic pulse upon hitting the ground, pulling all loose scrap and low-level enemies into the impact zone.

Level 14: Structural Reinforcement (Passive): Permanently increases maximum health by 15% and base physical defense by 10%.

Level 15: Polarity Shift (Active / Aura): Toggle ability. Drains 1 Scrap Charge per second. You project a magnetic field that passively deflects all metallic projectiles away from your body.

Level 16: Deflection Battery (Passive): Every projectile successfully deflected by Polarity Shift adds 1 hit to your combo multiplier.

Level 17: Wrecking Ball (Active): Consume 10 Scrap Charges to condense your collected metal into a massive ball on the end of your tether. Swing it in a 360-degree arc, instantly knocking down all surrounding enemies.

Level 18: Stripped Bare (Passive): Magnetic Tether now physically rips 10% of an enemy's armor rating off them permanently upon a successful pull.

Level 19: Deep Lacerations (Passive): Jagged Edges (Level 9) damage over time is increased by 50%.

Level 20: The Scrap-Storm (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Overload your magnetic gauntlets. For 5 seconds, all loose debris, dead enemy weapons, and dropped scrap in the arena violently swirl around you in a lethal vortex, damaging anyone who approaches. 35-second cooldown.

Tier 3: Advanced Mechanics & Survivability (Levels 21 - 30)

Level 21: Kinetic Shredder (Passive): Enemies caught inside The Scrap-Storm have their shields instantly broken and are launched into a jugglable state.

Level 22: Flawless Assembly (Passive): Reaching a 25-hit combo causes your Ratchet-Strikes to arc with static electricity, dealing 10% bonus shock damage.

Level 23: Perfect Assembly (Passive): Reaching a 50-hit combo allows your Junkyard Turret to fire piercing rounds, hitting multiple enemies in a straight line.

Level 24: Frame-Trap Decoy (Active): Dodge backward precisely as an enemy strikes to quickly assemble a crude, mechanical decoy of yourself. The enemy strikes the decoy, which explodes into shrapnel.

Level 25: Shrapnel Blindness (Passive): The explosion from Frame-Trap Decoy permanently blinds the attacker for 4 seconds, severely reducing their accuracy.

Level 26: Oil & Hydraulics (Passive): Permanently increases your stamina regeneration rate by 20%.

Level 27: Maximum Capacity (Passive): Scrap Charge storage capacity is increased from 20 to 40.

Level 28: Dual-Piston Overdrive (Active / Finisher): Consumes 20 Scrap Charges. Executes two hydraulic punches back-to-back. The second punch guarantees a critical hit and creates a directional shockwave.

Level 29: Scavenger’s Grace (Passive): Vaulting distance is increased by 15%, and vaulting over an enemy passively steals 1 Scrap Charge from their armor.

Level 30: The EMP Grid (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. Slam a high-voltage spike into the ground, emitting a massive electromagnetic pulse. Instantly stuns all biomechanical and tech-based enemies for 6 seconds and disables all enemy energy shields. 50-second cooldown.

Tier 4: Capstones & Mastery (Levels 31 - 40)

Level 31: System Reboot (Passive): Hitting enemies while they are stunned by the EMP Grid heals you for 2% of your maximum health per strike.

Level 32: Unbroken Machinery (Passive): Taking damage from an environmental hazard or trap no longer resets your combo multiplier.

Level 33: Critical Engineering (Passive): Base critical hit chance increased by 10% when attacking an enemy with no active shielding.

Level 34: Weak-Point Targeting (Passive): Critical hit damage increased by 20% against enemies suffering from Tetanus.

Level 35: The Master Mechanic (Aura): Consumes 30 Scrap Charges to activate. For 10 seconds, your Magnetic Tether has no cooldown, and your Junkyard Turrets no longer despawn, allowing you to build an entire automated firing squad on the field.

Level 36: Cooldown Reduction (Passive): Every successful Repulsor Parry reduces the cooldown of The Scrap-Storm and The EMP Grid by 1.5 seconds.

Level 37: Infinite Tether (Passive): You can now grapple to heavy enemies, launch off their chests, and instantly grapple to the next enemy mid-air indefinitely, creating a frictionless web of traversal.

Level 38: Kinetic Battery (Passive): Staying airborne for more than 5 seconds grants a stacking damage buff (2% per second) until you touch the floor.

Level 39: Emergency Defibrillator (Passive): When your health drops below 5%, your suit automatically delivers a massive electrical shock, restoring 30% of your health and stunning all enemies within a 5-meter radius. Can only occur once every 5 minutes.

Level 40: CAPSTONE - The Junkyard Titan (Active / Ultimate): Consumes a 100x combo multiplier to activate. You activate a master magnet. Every piece of scrap, every turret, and every dead enemy in the arena flies to your body, constructing a massive, 20-foot-tall mechanical mech-suit around you. For 15 seconds, you pilot this titan. Your health is completely shielded, your light attacks become wide-cleaving structural sweeps, and your heavy attack fires a concentrated beam of raw plasma that melts everything in its path.

7. The Kinetic Juggernaut
Combat Style: Heavy Bruiser / Unstoppable Momentum

Free-Flow Mechanic: The only class that does not have a standard dodge; instead, they absorb and redirect kinetic energy. By perfect-guarding incoming hits, they build a momentum charge. Once charged, their standard strikes become unstaggerable, allowing them to plow straight through enemy shields and interrupt massive boss attacks with sheer force.

Class 7 Architecture: The Kinetic Juggernaut
The immovable object and the unstoppable force. This class entirely discards standard evasion, boasting zero dodge mechanics. Instead, they absorb, store, and redirect incoming kinetic energy to plow through enemy ranks and shatter heavy armor.

Sub-Class 1: The Counter-Weight (Focuses on perfect guards, absorbing kinetic energy from enemy strikes, and releasing it in massive, singular blows).

Specialization A: Kinetic Absorption (Building charge by tanking hits, reflecting damage).

Specialization B: Release Valve (Expending all stored energy for catastrophic, one-hit-kill punches).

Sub-Class 2: The Momentum Engine (Focuses on building unstoppable speed and physically trampling fodder-class enemies).

Specialization A: The Stampede (Sprint-based combat, running through enemies to maintain flow).

Specialization B: Inertial Mass (The faster you move, the heavier you become, rendering you immune to knockbacks).

Sub-Class 3: The Seismic Brawler (Focuses on close-quarters grappling, heavy suplexes, and weaponizing the enemy's own body weight against them).

Specialization A: Heavy Grapple (Lifting and throwing Titan-class enemies, using them as battering rams).

Specialization B: Tectonic Slams (Jumping piledrivers that create localized earthquakes).

Sub-Class 4: The Inertia Bastion (Focuses on extreme armor plating, area denial, and taunting entire hordes to strike them).

Specialization A: Aggro Manipulation (Drawing all fire, creating safe zones for allies).

Specialization B: Reactive Armor (Spiked plating that instantly retaliates against melee attackers).

The Counter-Weight: Kinetic Absorption Specialization (Level 1 - 40)
This specialization tree requires nerves of steel. Instead of dodging unblockable attacks, you lean into them. By perfectly timing your Kinetic Guard, you absorb the devastating blows of massive bosses and immediately return the favor with double the force, completely dictating the flow of combat through sheer presence.

Tier 1: Foundation & The Wall (Levels 1 - 10)

Level 1: Heavy-Handed (Active): Your base light melee attack. Slower than other classes, but heavily resistant to being interrupted. Generates 1 Kinetic Charge (KC) per hit.

Level 2: The Kinetic Guard (Active): Replaces the standard dodge/roll button. Hold to brace yourself. Taking damage while bracing completely negates stagger and converts 50% of the incoming damage into 3 KC, but still drains a portion of your health.

Level 3: Perfect Deflection (Passive): Tapping the Kinetic Guard precisely as an attack lands completely negates all damage, staggers the attacker, and instantly fills 5 KC.

Level 4: Release Valve (Active / Finisher): Consumes 5 KC. A devastating, explosive gut-punch that physically launches the target backward, shattering all frontal shields.

Level 5: Unstoppable Force (Passive): While executing Release Valve, you gain Hyper-Armor and cannot be staggered or interrupted by any attack in the game.

Level 6: Vaulting Stomp (Active): Unlocks directional vault. Because of your mass, vaulting over an enemy violently stomps on their shoulders, instantly dropping them to the floor in a prone state.

Level 7: Momentum Decay (Passive): Your combo decay timer is 25% longer than other classes, compensating for your slower movement speed.

Level 8: Uppercut Transfer (Active): Holding the heavy attack button unleashes a kinetic uppercut. Only launches lightweight enemies, but leaves heavy enemies severely staggered.

Level 9: Shock Absorption (Passive): For every KC you currently hold, you gain a flat 1% physical damage reduction (caps at 10%).

Level 10: The Haymaker (Active / Cooldown): Major Ability. You plant your feet, charge for 1 second, and dash straight forward in a 10-meter line. Anything caught in your path is violently thrown aside and takes massive blunt-force damage. 20-second cooldown.

Tier 2: Combo Scaling & Retaliation (Levels 11 - 20)

Level 11: Aerial Weight (Passive): While you cannot jump as high as other classes, your mid-air attacks deal 20% more damage due to your extreme mass.

Level 12: Crowd Clearing (Passive): Release Valve (Level 4) now projects a short-range, cone-shaped shockwave behind the primary target, damaging tightly grouped enemies.

Level 13: Crater Drop (Active): Mid-air, press the heavy attack button to plummet straight down like a stone, creating a kinetic shockwave that knocks surrounding enemies completely off their feet.

Level 14: Thick-Skinned (Passive): Permanently increases maximum health by 25%.
